I arrived at the hotel early and had no trouble checking in, the staff, particularly Zero were very helpful and always happy to assist me if they could.

The room is all clean and comfortable, when I checked in they told me that there's construction happening, this turned out to not be an issue and was very well managed to reduce noise. The only bit of construction I heard was some drilling for about 5 minutes.

Whilst at the hotel I decided to splurge a little and book a massage, this was a lovely way to end a long day,  the masseuse was very professional. 

Getting to the hotel from the airport is super easy as the hotel is adjacent to the subway station that goes to the airport.

overall, great stay would stay again.
